  126. I have been on the hunt for a new moisturizer for the last several months since my favorite moisturizer has been discontinued. I decided to try Garnier Moisture Rescue Refreshing Gel-Cream because it had good reviews on Amazon. I have never previously used a Garnier product or a gel moisturizer before. Unfortunately, this moisturizer isn't for me and it is largely because of the scent.<br /><br />A rundown on my skin type. I have very sensitive skin. I tend to have combination skin, although when my skin is dry it is VERY dry. It it gets oily it just gets moderately oily. I don't really have issues with breakouts (only a pimple here or there from time to time), but do have issues with my skin breaking out into a itching rash.<br /><br />When I purchased this moisturizer I was hoping for a light-weight, oil-free, scent-free moisturizer. I wanted something that didn't leave my skin feeling oily, but also moisturized it. Also, having very sensitive skin I need a moisturizer that won't cause pimple breakouts or rash breakouts. Lastly, I need a moisturizer that I can put my liquid foundation over and still gives me an even skin tone. Although the Garnier Moisture Rescue Refreshing Gel-Cream lived up to a lot of these requirements I had big enough issues that this product just isn't going to work.<br /><br />I've previously never used a gel moisturizer before. This was the first time and I have to say I wouldn't be opposed to it in the future. I don't know why they call it a gel-cream as there is nothing cream about it. This moisturizing gel is very similar to putting aloe on your face. The consistency of the gel is very similar to aloe and it soaks into your skin relatively quickly like aloe.<br /><br />I had limited use of this product so I am not exactly sure how it would have panned out in terms of overall moisturizing my skin and skin breakouts. In the two weeks I used it I did not suffer from any skin irritation or pimple breakouts. Also, it left my skin feeling very soft. For the most part my skin felt moisturized and being a gel it was very light-weight and non-greasy.<br /><br />Ultimately, the problem I had with this product is it is scented. The scent is light, but per-fumy. Scented skin products are never good for someone with sensitive skin (or sensitive anything for that matter). The scent never went away until I washed the moisturizer off my face. It followed me around all day and being on my face it was so close to my nose. I also had issues with my eyes drying out from the smell. At first I wasn't sure why my eyes were drying out and thought it might have to do with the moisturizer. I stopped using the moisturizer and I stopped having issues with my eyes drying out.<br /><br />Product Pros:<br />- It moisturizes your skin.<br />- Lightweight<br />- Oil-free<br />- Leaves skin smooth feeling.<br />- No breakouts or skin irritation.<br /><br />Product Cons:<br />- Has too much of a scent.<br />- Irritated my eyes.<br /><br />Overall, I will not be purchasing this moisturizer again in the future. If they decide to make an unscented version I absolutely would be interested in trying it again.<br /><br />Side Note: One thing I've learned having life long issues with sensitive skin is what doesn't work for one person could work fabulous for another and visa versa. So sadly, unless everyone is saying its horrible, you might have to try it out for yourself to find out it if is the right product for you. Everyone's skin is different and reacts differently to products.

  247. For context, I've tried a few Garnier products and have found them to be generally very good, with the Skin Renew moisturizer currently a part of my daily morning routine. The descriptions and most of the reviews seemed to indicate that this gel-cream fit the bill, but after about a week of daily a.m./p.m. use I'm a bit disappointed. First, the texture was off-putting -- not unpleasant, per se, but when a skin care product is packaged in a jar, you expect it to have a thicker, more viscous consistency (especially when it's labeled a gel-CREAM). This product looks and feels almost like un-set jell-o that was taken out of the fridge way, way, WAY too early. Not sure if somehow the jar I received came from an \\"off\\" batch, but my first thought is that it should have been packaged in a bottle with a pump dispenser. On the plus side, the product absorbs quickly into skin without feeling greasy or leaving a lasting residue. Also, it has a pleasant fragrance, though I wouldn't mind a lighter concentration of the scent. It did, however, make my irritated patches sting upon contact. And while my skin did feel refreshed, the hydration certainly didn't last 24 hours as the description claims (even with consistent a.m. and p.m. use for a week). At best, I'd say the feeling of being moisturized lasts a couple hours. In short, for the purpose of gentle yet intense moisturization (the reason I originally sought this product out), I'm not sure I'd buy this again. On the other hand, if my skin were to calm down and return to my normal, nonsensitive oily/combo-type complexion, this product might be worth a second look.
